Each franchisee of an ‚ÄúAtomic Wings‚Äù franchise will license directly from us the right to operate a quick service restaurant in a casual environment under the mark ‚ÄúAtomic Wings‚Äù that provides on-premises dining as well as carry-out and delivery services (‚ÄúFranchised Restaurant‚Äù). The Franchised Restaurants offer Buffalo-style chicken wings that are hormone free, antibiotic free, and halal served in varying degrees of spiciness; appetizers; burgers; sandwiches; chili; soups; Mexican food; and desserts in accordance with specified recipes and procedures ("Menu Items") which may be changed by us from time to time. With our prior written approval, the Franchised Restaurants may offer additional menu items like gyros, falafel and chicken over rice and if permitted by applicable law, may serve beer and wine. The total investment necessary to begin operation of an Atomic Wings area representative business is $119,750 to $332,500. This includes $100,000 and $150,000 that must be paid to the franchisor or its affiliate. Graze Craze is an innovator in the food trend sweeping the nation known as ‚ÄúGrazing‚Äù. Grazing allows people the flexibility to eat an entire meal or small portions of food during the course of the day. The grazing style of eating provides you and your guests with a diverse meal plan in the form of a charcuterie style grazing box, platter or table that meets the individual needs and wants of everyone's personal palette and diet, in relation to those who may have special health or medical eating requirements.
